number): number | null {\n  if (!Number.isFinite(gestationalWeek)) {\n    return null;\n  }\n\n  const sorted = FETAL_WEIGHT_REFERENCE_POINTS;\n  if (gestationalWeek <= sorted[0]!.week) {\n    return sorted[0]!.grams;\n  }\n  if (gestationalWeek >= sorted[sorted.length - 1]!.week) {\n    return sorted[sorted.length - 1]!.grams;\n  }\n\n  for (let index = 0; index < sorted.length - 1; index += 1) action: RetentionAction;\n    dataCategory: RetentionDataCategory;\n    id: string;\n    retentionDays: number;\n  };\n  tenantId: string;\n}) {\n  const retentionExecutionModel = readRetentionModel<RetentionExecutionDelegate>(\"dataRetentionExecution\");\n  const cutoff = new Date(Date.now() - input.policy.retentionDays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);\n  let affectedCount = 0;\n  let scannedCount = 0;\n\n  switch (input.policy.dataCategory) {\n    case RETENTION_DATA_CATEGORY.OUTPUT_ARTIFACTS: {\n      const where = {\n        createdAt: {\n          lt: cutoff\n        },\n      where\n        });\n        affectedCount = result.count;\n      }\n      break;\n    }\n    case RETENTION_DATA_CATEGORY.LOGIN_ALERTS: {\n      const where = {\n        createdAt: {\n          lt: cutoff\n        },\n        organizationId: input.organizationId\n      };\n      scannedCount = await prisma.loginAlert.count({ where });\n\n      if (input.mode !== RETENTION_EXECUTION_MODE.DRY_RUN && scannedCount > 0) {\n        const result = await prisma.loginAlert.deleteMany({ where });\n        affectedCount = result.count;\n      }\n      break;\n    }\n    case RETENTION_DATA_CATEGORY.MFA_CHALLENGES: {\n      const where = {\n        createdAt: {\n          lt: cutoff\n        },\n        organizationId: input.organizationId\n      };\n      scannedCount = await prisma.mfaChallenge.count({ where });\n\n      if (input.mode !== RETENTION_EXECUTION_MODE.DRY_RUN && scannedCount > 0) {\n        const result = await prisma.mfaChallenge.deleteMany({ where });\n        affectedCount = result.count;\n      }\n      break;\n    }\n    case RETENTION_DATA_CATEGORY.MFA_RECOVERY_CODES: {\n      const where = {\n        OR: [\n          {\n            createdAt: {\n              lt: cutoff\n            }\n          },\n          {\n            usedAt: {\n              lt: cutoff\n            }\n          }\n        ],\n        tenantId: input.tenantId\n      };\n      scannedCount = await prisma.mfaRecoveryCode.count({ where });\n\n      if (input.mode !== RETENTION_EXECUTION_MODE.DRY_RUN && scannedCount > 0) {\n        const result = await prisma.mfaRecoveryCode.deleteMany({ where });\n        affectedCount = result.count;\n      }\n      break;\n    }\n    case RETENTION_DATA_CATEGORY.SUSPENDED_USERS: {\n      const users = await listSuspendedUsersForRetention({\n        organizationId: input.organizationId,\n        cutoff\n      });\n      scannedCount = users.length;\n\n      if (input.mode !== RETENTION_EXECUTION_MODE.DRY_RUN && users.length > 0) {\n        await Promise.all(\n          users.map(async (user) => {\n            await prisma.user.update({\n              data: {\n                email: anonymizedEmail(user.id),\n                mfaEnabled: false,\n                mfaFailedAttempts: 0,\n                mfaLockedUntil: null,\n                mfaSecret: null,\n                name: \"Deleted User\",\n                passwordHash: await hashPassword(randomToken(18), {\n                  memoryKiB: input.config.AUTH_ARGON2_MEMORY_KIB,\n                  parallelism: input.config.AUTH_ARGON2_PARALLELISM,\n                  passes: input.config.AUTH_ARGON2_PASSES\n                })\n              },\n              where: {\n                id: user.id\n              }\n            });\n          })\n        );\n        affectedCount = users.length;\n      }\n      break;\n    }\n    default:\n      break;\n  }\n\n  const execution = await retentionExecutionModel.create({\n    data: {\n      action: input.policy.action,\n      dataCategory: input.policy.dataCategory,\n      mode: input.mode,\n      organizationId: input.organizationId,\n      policyId: input.policy.id,\n      scannedCount,\n      affectedCount,\n      tenantId: input.tenantId\n    }\n  });\n\n  await prisma.auditLog.create({\n    data: {\n      action: \"privacy.retention.executed\",\n      diff: {\n        after: {\n          action: input.policy.action,\n          affectedCount,\n          dataCategory: input.policy.dataCategory,\n          mode: input.mode,\n          scannedCount\n        },\n        before: {}\n      },\n      entityId: execution.id,\n      entityType: \"data_retention_execution\",\n      tenantId: input.tenantId\n    }\n  });\n\n  return {\n    affectedCount,\n    dataCategory: input.policy.dataCategory,\n    executionId: execution.id,\n    scannedCount\n  };\n}\n\nexport async function listRetentionPolicies(input: {\n  organizationReference: string;\n}) {\n  const retentionExecutionModel = readRetentionModel<RetentionExecutionDelegate>(\"dataRetentionExecution\");\n  const explicitTrigger?.key ?? canvas.steps[0]!.key;\n}\n\nfunction createWebhookSecret(identity: ScopedIdentity, workflowName: string): string {\n  return createHash(\"sha256\")\n    .update(`${identity.tenantId}:${workflowName}:${Date.now()}:${randomUUID()}`)\n    .digest(\"hex\");\n}\n\nasync function persistCanvas(\n  client: WorkflowWriteClient,\n  identity: ScopedIdentity,\n  workflowId: string,\n  canvas: WorkflowCanvas\n): Promise<void> {\n  const stepIdByKey = new Map<string, string>();\n\n  for (const step of canvas.steps) {\n    const created = await client.workflowStep.create({\n      data: {\n        config: step.config as Prisma.InputJsonValue,\n        isTrigger:\n          step.type === \"TRIGGER_WEBHOOK\" ||\n          step.type === \"TRIGGER_CRON\" ||\n          step.type === \"TRIGGER_EVENT\",\n        key: step.key,\n        name: step.name,\n        organizationId: identity.organizationId,\n        tenantId: identity.tenantId,\n        type: step.type,\n        workflowId\n      }\n    });\n\n    stepIdByKey.set(step.key, created.id);\n  }\n\n  for (const transition of canvas.transitions) {\n    const updateWorkflowInScope(\n  config: ApiConfig,\n  workflowId: string,\n  identity: ScopedIdentity,\n  input: WorkflowUpdateInput,\n  existingWorkflow?: WorkflowRecord\n): Promise<WorkflowRecord> {\n  const existing = existingWorkflow ?? (await getWorkflowById(workflowId, identity.tenantId));\n  if (!existing) {\n    throw new Error(\"WORKFLOW_NOT_FOUND\");\n  }\n\n  if (input.canvas) {\n    ensureCanvasIsDag(input.canvas);\n  }\n\n WorkflowStatus.PUBLISHED) {\n      workflowUpdateData.archivedAt = null;\n      workflowUpdateData.publishedAt = new Date();\n      workflowUpdateData.status = WorkflowStatus.PUBLISHED;\n    } else if (input.status === WorkflowStatus.DRAFT) {\n      workflowUpdateData.archivedAt = null;\n      workflowUpdateData.publishedAt = null;\n      workflowUpdateData.status = WorkflowStatus.DRAFT;\n    }\n\n    if (input.cronExpression !== undefined) {\n      workflowUpdateData.cronExpression = input.cronExpression;\n    }\n\n    if (input.canvas !== undefined) {\n      workflowUpdateData.definition = input.canvas as Prisma.InputJsonValue;\n    }\n\n    if (input.description !== undefined) {\n      workflowUpdateData.description = input.description;\n    }\n\n    if (input.eventTopic !== undefined) {\n      workflowUpdateData.eventTopic = input.eventTopic;\n    }\n\n    if (input.maxDepth !== undefined) {\n      workflowUpdateData.maxDepth = input.maxDepth;\n    }\n\n    if (input.name !== undefined) {\n      workflowUpdateData.name = input.name;\n    }\n\n    if (input.triggerConfig !== undefined) {\n      workflowUpdateData.triggerConfig = input.triggerConfig as Prisma.InputJsonValue;\n    }\n\n    if (input.triggerType !== undefined) {\n      workflowUpdateData.triggerType = input.triggerType;\n    }\n\n    if (input.canvas) {\n      workflowUpdateData.version = { increment: 1 };\n    }\n\n    const workflow = await tx.workflow.update({\n      data: workflowUpdateData,\n      where: {\n        id: workflowId\n      }\n    });\n\n    if (input.canvas) {\n      await tx.workflowRevision.create({\n        data: {\n          definition: input.canvas as Prisma.InputJsonValue,\n          organizationId: identity.organizationId,\n resolveResumeStepKey(input: {\n  execution: NonNullable<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof prisma.workflowExecution.findFirst>>>;\n  requestedStepKey?: string | undefined;\n  workflowId: string;\n}): Promise<string> {\n  if (input.requestedStepKey) {\n    return input.requestedStepKey;\n  }\n\n  const latestFailedStep = await prisma.stepResult.findFirst({\n    include: {\n      step: true\n    },\n    orderBy: {\n      createdAt: \"desc\"\n    },\n    where: {\n      executionId: input.execution.id,\n      status: \"FAILED\",\n      workflowId: input.workflowId\n    }\n  });\n\n  if depth: number;\n  resumeStepKey: string;\n  resumedFromExecutionId: string;\n}> {\n  const sourceExecution = await prisma.workflowExecution.findFirst({\n    where: {\n      id: WorkflowExecutionStatus.FAILED) {\n    throw new ProblemDetailsError({\n      detail: \"Only failed executions can be resumed from a checkpoint.\",\n      status: 409,\n      title: \"Conflict\"\n function cloneCheckpointResults(input: {\n  client: Pick<WorkflowTransactionClient, \"stepResult\">;\n  executionId: string;\n  fromExecutionId: string;\n  fromStepKey: string;\n  organizationId:
